Cookies, web beacons and IP address.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E A cookie is a piece of data stored locally on your computer, which contains information about your activities on the Internet. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Application.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EOn the Application, we use cookies to track users progress through the Application, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Application to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Application and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EOnce you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EIf you continue to use our Application we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EIf you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Application. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the Application and see public pages thereon.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EA web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Application that delivers a small graphic image from another Application or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EWe use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EPlease note, any interaction with the Application may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. We may use your (IP) address to help diagnose problems with our Application, to administer the Application, or to gather demographic information about our Users. Your IP address may also be used to assist in the detection of fraud and we may pass this information to the legal bodies for that purpose.\n    If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or would like to have access to your data, please contact our Data Protection Officer at \u003Ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"mailto:support@dreamteam.gg\"\u003Esupport@dreamteam.gg.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\n\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\n    Revision: 10 April 2019","FORTNITE.PAGE.PRIVACY_POLICY":"Privacy Policy Agreement","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.ANDROID":"Android","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.CONSOLE":"Gamepad","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.IOS":"iOS","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.PC":"Keyboard","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.PS4":"PS4","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.SWITCH":"Nintendo Switch","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.TOUCH":"Touch","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.X1":"XBox","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.XB1":"XBox","FORTNITE.PRIVACY.PRIVACY_CONTENT":"Privacy Policy\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      1. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Website.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      On the Website, we use cookies to track users progress through the Website, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Website to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Website and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      Once you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      If you continue to use our Website we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      If you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Website. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the website and see public pages thereon.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      A web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Website that delivers a small graphic image from another website or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      We use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      Please note, any interaction with the Website may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. Cookies, web beacons and IP address.\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E A cookie is a piece of data stored locally on your computer, which contains information about your activities on the Internet. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Platform. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E On the Platform, we use cookies to track users progress through the Platform, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Platform to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Platform and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E Once you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E If you continue to use our Platform we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E If you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Platform. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the website and see public pages thereon. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E A web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Platform that delivers a small graphic image from another website or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E We use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E Please note, any interaction with the Platform may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. We may use your (IP) address to help diagnose problems with our Platform, to administer the Platform, or to gather demographic information about our Users. Your IP address may also be used to assist in the detection of fraud and we may pass this information to the legal bodies for that purpose. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or would like to have access to your data, please contact our Data Protection Officer at&nbsp;\u003Ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"mailto:support@dreamteam.gg\" class=\"underline\"\u003Esupport@dreamteam.gg\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n     \u003Cli\u003E Thank you! \u003Cbr\u003E \u003Cstrong\u003ERevision: 25 May 2018\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E \u003Cp\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n   \u003C\u002Ful\u003E","PROFILE.ABOUT.ABOUT_ME":"About Me","PROFILE.ABOUT.AGE":"Age","PROFILE.ABOUT.GENDER":"Gender","PROFILE.ABOUT.LANGUAGES":"Languages","PROFILE.ABOUT.YEARS_OLD":"yo","PROFILE.CHAT_BUTTON":"CHAT","PROFILE.SETTINGS":"Settings","SOCIAL.LFG.SEARCH.DESCRIPTION":"Friends offline? It encrypts all of your Personal Data granted to us, so we believe that it cannot be read by third parties); and\n    \u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n    \u003Cli\u003E\n      Accountability: we will be responsible for and be able to demonstrate compliance with the above-mentioned principles.\n    \u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n    \u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n    \u003Cb\u003E7. Cookies, web beacons and IP address.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E A cookie is a piece of data stored locally on your computer, which contains information about your activities on the Internet. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Application.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EOn the Application, we use cookies to track users progress through the Application, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Application to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Application and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EOnce you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EIf you continue to use our Application we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EIf you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Application. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the Application and see public pages thereon.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EA web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Application that delivers a small graphic image from another Application or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EWe use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you.\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003EPlease note, any interaction with the Application may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. We may use your (IP) address to help diagnose problems with our Application, to administer the Application, or to gather demographic information about our Users. Your IP address may also be used to assist in the detection of fraud and we may pass this information to the legal bodies for that purpose.\n    If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or would like to have access to your data, please contact our Data Protection Officer at \u003Ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"mailto:support@dreamteam.gg\"\u003Esupport@dreamteam.gg.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\n\n    \u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\u003Cbr\u002F\u003E\n    Revision: 10 April 2019","FORTNITE.PAGE.PRIVACY_POLICY":"Privacy Policy Agreement","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.ANDROID":"Android","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.CONSOLE":"Gamepad","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.IOS":"iOS","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.PC":"Keyboard","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.PS4":"PS4","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.SWITCH":"Nintendo Switch","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.TOUCH":"Touch","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.X1":"XBox","FORTNITE.PLATFORM_ICON.XB1":"XBox","FORTNITE.PRIVACY.PRIVACY_CONTENT":"Privacy Policy\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      1. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Website.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      On the Website, we use cookies to track users progress through the Website, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Website to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Website and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      Once you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      If you continue to use our Website we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      If you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Website. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the website and see public pages thereon.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      A web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Website that delivers a small graphic image from another website or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      We use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      Please note, any interaction with the Website may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. We may use your (IP) address to help diagnose problems with our Website, to administer the Website, or to gather demographic information about our Users. Your IP address may also be used to assist in the detection of fraud and we may pass this information to the legal bodies for that purpose.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or would like to have access to your data, please contact our Data Protection Officer at \u003Ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"mailto:support@dreamteam.gg\" class=\"underline\"\u003Esupport@dreamteam.gg.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n      Thank you! Cookies, web beacons and IP address.\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E A cookie is a piece of data stored locally on your computer, which contains information about your activities on the Internet. The information in a cookie does not contain any personally identifiable information you submit to the Platform. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E On the Platform, we use cookies to track users progress through the Platform, allowing us to make improvements based on usage data. We also use cookies if you log in to the Platform to enable you to remain logged in. A cookie helps you to get the best out of the Platform and helps us to provide you with a more customised Service. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E Once you close your browser, our access to the cookie terminates. You have the ability to accept or decline cookies. Most web browsers automatically accept cookies, but you can usually modify your browser setting to decline cookies if you prefer. To change your browser settings, you should go to your advanced preferences. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E If you continue to use our Platform we assume you agree to our use of cookies as described above. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E If you choose not to accept the cookies, this will not affect your access to the majority of information available on the Platform. However, you will not be able to make full use of our online Services and even log-in into your Account and use your Personal Data therefrom, but however you will be able to browse through the website and see public pages thereon. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E A web beacon, also referred to as a clear gif or page tag, consists of code on the Platform that delivers a small graphic image from another website or third-party server. They may not be visible as the beacon is generally a 1x1 pixel that is often designed to blend into the background of a webpage. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E We use web beacons, often in conjunction with cookies, to monitor the effectiveness of ad banners; and to gather general log, statistical, and referral information. We do not use beacons to store or link to Personal Data. We thus use beacons to understand certain actions that you took (such as a purchase), but not to identify you. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \u003Cp\u003E Please note, any interaction with the Platform may reveal your Internet protocol (IP) address. We may use your (IP) address to help diagnose problems with our Platform, to administer the Platform, or to gather demographic information about our Users. The problem is that most non-gamers have no clue. This year, DreamTeam has created a list of perfect stocking stuffers. You still have time to drop some hints. \n&nbsp;\nDUCO Video Gaming Glasses Blue Light Blocking Glasses, $25\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nRealistically, you should take frequent screen breaks to give your eyes a rest. And much more.\n&nbsp;\nRetro Arcade Handheld Gaming System, $24\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nIf introducing a full-sized arcade cabinet into your home is too much, go for a handheld version. This one comes pre-loaded with 200 games. \n&nbsp;\nDualShock 4 Charging Station for PS4, $17\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nBecause nothing sucks more than losing power in the middle of an epic run. Arcade1Up even sells matching stools.\n&nbsp;\nFortnite T-Shirt, $20\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nHigh quality Fortnite inspired T-Shirts by independent artists and designers from around the world.\n&nbsp;\nCopper-Infused Fingerless Compression Gloves, $21\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThese gloves work like compression sleeves that help improve circulation to the affected limbs, reducing inflammation, and providing a gamer with longer-lasting pain relief. The Copper Joint also aids in the more efficient rehabilitation of the efficient joints so you can resume your computer gaming activities.\n&nbsp;\nVideo Games Collection Puzzle, $20\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nPuzzles: the original gaming. Help yourself set some goals and see how you measure up to the most impressive video game records in the world.\n&nbsp;\nSnowball USB Microphone, $68\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nAnother one for the streamers, because the audio quality should be as on point as the visuals. Blue&#8217;s Snowball doesn&#8217;t just look cool; it captures crystal-clear sound. With USB, getting started is as simple as plugging in.\n&nbsp;\nCustom Xbox Controller, $80\n\n&nbsp;\nWith full-color customization, this is a creative way to give your Xbox gamer a one-of-a-kind gift.\n&nbsp;\nKingTop Mechanical Gaming Keyboard, $30\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nYou can choose to present an ordinary keyboard, or you can go full mechanical. And if you do choose the latter, make sure to get the KingTop Mechanical Gaming Keyboard. You&#8217;d be amazed at the backlight effects, utilizing six different colors to provide you with a visual experience to go with the tactile sensations of the fully mechanical keys. Each of the 104 keys on this keyboard has been rigorously tested for strength, durability, and responsiveness, while also ensuring its water resistance.\n&nbsp;\nHAVIT Wired Mouse, $11\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nIt may not have a very remarkable optical sensor that can run in the 16,000s, but its maximum of 3,200 DPI should be enough to provide any player with exceptional gaming experience. Its DPI setting can be adjusted to three other levels with the lowest at 800 DPI. The Havit mouse also comes with breathing LED light effects, including seven circular, LED light effects to set the mood in your game.\n&nbsp;\nAtlantic Gaming Desk, $92\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe Atlantic gaming desk is a piece of steel furniture that&#8217;s specially built for today&#8217;s modern gamer or even a home office owner. There is a charge station, a monitor stand, game storage rank, game controller hooks, gaming speaker trays, and a whole lot more. \n&nbsp;\nHandheld Retro Game Console Phone Case, $16\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nChances are, the gamer you&#8217;re shopping for has owned a Game Boy at some point in their life. This nostalgia-inducing, Game Boy-inspired case actually has functional buttons and a screen on it for playing video games. Your recipient will be able to play games like Tetris, Pac-Man, and Super Mario Bros. The case will also let you wirelessly charge your phone, and it is powered by a rechargeable battery.\n&nbsp;\nPlaystation Alarm Clock, $30\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nHelp your gamer friend start their adventure off on the right foot with help from this PlayStation alarm clock  because let&#8217;s face it, much as they love reality, they&#8217;d much rather live in a video game 24\u002F7. And this is one step closer to that! It looks just like their DualShock 4 controller, has an easy-to-read backlit display, and is powered by a USB cable.\n&nbsp;\nNintendo Patent Posters (Set of 4 8&#215;10 Unframed Prints), $19\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThis artwork of four patents captures the innovative spirit behind everyone&#8217;s favorite old school Nintendo consoles. The prints will look incredible in any game room. They&#8217;re printed on Fuji Crystal Archive paper, which doesn&#8217;t feel flimsy. \n&nbsp;\nPlayStation VR Starter Pack, $288\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nGot a PS4 but not yet on board with virtual reality? Dive head-first into PSVR with this kit comprising the headset, PS Camera, and a copy of PlayStation VR Worlds. Our tip: pick up a pair of PlayStation Move controllers too, which aren&#8217;t included in this kit.\n \nXbox One X, $365\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThis is the Microsoft equivalent to the PlayStation 4 Pro and offers similar upgrades to performance and picture resolution. It&#8217;s a bigger leap than between Sony&#8217;s two console models though and is currently the most powerful console in the world, which obviously has a big appeal to gamers  although equally obviously it&#8217;s quite expensive.\n \nLogitech Racing Wheel + Pedals, $237\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe best part about most controllers these days is that they work with their respective console and the PC. Others are more difficult, like Squad Goals, which requires you to win 100 Season 1 Squad matches or even something like Rise &amp; Grind, which you&#8217;ll only get if you hit level 250 this season.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EIn any case, here&#8217;s the full list. Check out \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Ffortnite\u002Fchallenges?region[]=america&amp;status[]=active&amp;status[]=soon\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"\u003EFortnite challenges\u003C\u002Fa\u003E on DreamTeam.gg. And earn some cash for some of those new emotes.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe post \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Ffortnite-chapter-2-season-1-all-you-need-to-know-before-season-2\u002F\"\u003EFortnite Chapter 2 Season 1: All You Need To Know Before Season 2\u003C\u002Fa\u003E appeared first on \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\"\u003EDreamTeam Blog\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n","content_text":"There are a bunch of changes in Fortnite: Chapter 2, including graphical and sound improvements, new and newly vaulted weapons, boats, the ability to swim, and even an entirely new map.\n&nbsp;\nChapter 2 introduces tons of new features to Fortnite: Battle Royale, including a new island map with 13 locations to explore. You&#8217;ll also be able to play around in the water in new ways, with support for swimming, fishing, and motorboats.\n&nbsp;\nBut one of the coolest changes is something that the game has needed ever since it launched.\n&nbsp;\nThe new map is the biggest change\n&nbsp;\nWhen you drop out of the Battle Bus for the first time, you immediately see that Epic hasn&#8217;t uncovered the names of the new map locations. That&#8217;s an intentional part of Epic&#8217;s new medal system, which exists alongside challenges. It rewards you for completing various in-game activities, like finding and visiting some of the 13 new landmarks dotted around the new island. Some old points of interest  like Retail Row and Salty Springs  have also made the jump, giving players the option of returning to their favorite jump spots.\n&nbsp;\nBoats boats boats\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThere&#8217;s also now motorboats for zooming around in, giving several new ways to navigate the island. \n&nbsp;\nFewer guns\n&nbsp;\nThere&#8217;s a streamlined arsenal of weaponry this time around, no doubt to keep things simple at the outset of Season 1. Mainstays like the Pickaxe and Assault Rifle remain.\n&nbsp;\nBetter graphics\n&nbsp;\nFortnite Chapter 2 also comes with a visual upgrade, with cleaner and more vivid graphics throughout. Fortnite streamer DrLupo said that &#8220;The graphics genuinely makes it look like a brand new game&#8221;.\n&nbsp;\nLevel cap is gone\n&nbsp;\nOther new additions include the removal of the level cap, meaning those of you at Level 100 can continue earning XP. We&#8217;re not currently sure what the new cap is, but 250 seems like an obvious choice.\n&nbsp;\nShoot health\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nOne incredible addition is a new health bazooka  the Bandage Bazooka, to be exact  revives your fallen squad members, putting friendly fire in a whole new light. There&#8217;s also a new set of emotes for high-fiving or synchronizing dance moves together  meaning you never have to floss alone again.\n&nbsp;\nWays to hide, and things to blow up\n&nbsp;\nIn classic Assassin&#8217;s Creed style, you&#8217;ll even be able to hide in hay bales (or dumpsters), while &#8220;gas tanks and explosive barrels&#8221; will make for some exciting environmental dangers.\n&nbsp;\nAddition of achievements\n&nbsp;\nOne of the other significant changes in Fortnite Chapter 2 is the addition of achievements. There are a total of 52 achievements to unlock, and some of them are a bit more obvious than others.\n&nbsp;\nFor instance, the Double Trouble achievement is unlocked by winning 10 Season 1 Duo matches. However, the &#8220;I&#8217;m Trash&#8221; achievement is unlocked by . . . Well, it says &#8220;Just the worst&#8221; so we&#8217;re not quite sure. Though we suppose we have some matches that almost certainly qualify.\n  \nSome of these are super easy like &#8220;In the Zone,&#8221; which only requires you to land in the starting safe zone. Others are more difficult, like Squad Goals, which requires you to win 100 Season 1 Squad matches or even something like Rise &amp; Grind, which you&#8217;ll only get if you hit level 250 this season.\n&nbsp;\nIn any case, here&#8217;s the full list. You can view the achievements in the Career Tab in-game.\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nIn any case, here&#8217;s the full list. You can view the achievements in the Career Tab in-game:\n&nbsp;\n&#8211; Hide the Pain  Used a Bandage to heal yourself while in the storm.\n&#8211; Pier Fishing  Caught a fish off the Sweaty Sands pier.\n&#8211; Can I speak to a Manager?  Took out your frustrations on 20 Fishstick restaurant decorations.\n&#8211; All You Can Eat Sashimi  Ate all the fish and two plastic lobsters.\n&#8211; Let Yourself Down  Eliminate yourself by fall damage.\n&#8211; Collecting Rust  Harvested 999 Metal in a single match.\n&#8211; I&#8217;m Trash  Just the worst.\n&#8211; In the Zone  Landed inside the starting safe zone.\n&#8211; Who&#8217;s a Good Doggo?  You&#8217;re a good doggo. Yes, you are!\n&#8211; Were You Raised in a Barn!?  Got revived inside the Frenzy Farm barn.\n&#8211; Double Trouble  Won 10 Duos matches during Season 1.\n&#8211; Champion!  Won 10 Solo matches during Season 1.\n&#8211; Squad Goals  Won 100 Squads matches during Season 1.\n&#8211; Cabin Fever  You&#8217;ve been in this cabin for a long time.\n&#8211; Mission Complete!  Completed all Missions during Season 1.\n&#8211; Bushwacker  Destroyed 500 Holly Hedges.\n&#8211; Trophy Hunter  Eliminated an opponent with a Mythic Goldfish.\n&#8211; Tourist Trap  Eliminated an opponent with a Trap in Misty Meadows.\n&#8211; You&#8217;ve Hit a Brick Wall  Harvested 999 Stone in a single match.\n&#8211; Hittin&#8217; the Hay  Hid in the hay.\n&#8211; Salt Bae  Been droppin&#8217; Salty.\n&#8211; Desperate Times  You picked up a Common Pistol.\n&#8211; A Kick in the Grass  Scored a goal in the Pleasant Park soccer field.\n&#8211; Two Can Play That Game  Won 100 Duos matches during Season 1.\n&#8211; Victorious!  Won 100 Solo matches during Season 1.\n&#8211; Team Player  Won a Team Rumble match during Season 1.\n&#8211; Carrying the Team  You carried a teammate for 50 meters.\n&#8211; On A Mission!  Completed your first Season 1 Mission.\n&#8211; WARNING!  Slurpfish contain 4,000% of your daily recommended toxic waste.\n&#8211; Quick &amp; Dirty  Eliminated an opponent in Dirty Docks within 60 seconds of jumping from the Battle Bus.\n&#8211; Submarine Submachine  Eliminated an opponent with an SMG while in water.\n&#8211; Woodchuck  Harvested 999 Wood in a single match.\n&#8211; Got &#8216;Em! And on top of that, DreamTeams profiles have a new feature that can help stop the growing level of toxicity in the gaming community. Is that even possible, you ask? Yep, find out how below! Or, skip the reading and experience your Player Profile now!\n&nbsp;\nNew Profile\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe new Player Profiles are divided into four sections: Personality, Games, Achievements, and Activity. Lets take a look at each one. \n&nbsp;\nPersonality\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe personality section showcases who you are as a gamer. It includes:\n&#8211; Some basic info about yourself. \n&#8211; A quote  Be sure to add something inspirational or funny. \n&#8211; Connect social platforms (Discord, Mixer, Twitch, Twitter, and YouTube)  get more subscribers and views. \n&#8211; Toxicity control  Other gamers can now rate and review you as a gamer. So, play nice!\n&nbsp;\nThis information can be added or updated in the player settings: \n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nGames\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe games section allows you to connect the games you play. DreamTeam currently only supports Apex Legends, CS:GO, Fortnite, and LoL. Call of Duty: Modern Warfare will be supported soon, really soon, like four days.  Once you connect your game, youll be able to click on that game to view all of your stats and see your progress. \n&nbsp;\nSEE ALL GAMES\n&nbsp;\nAchievements\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe achievement section shows off your Challenge Badges. This is home to true skill. In fact, our writer had to photoshop this image as he simply isnt good enough to have anything other than the Challenge Accepted badge. Haha. \n&nbsp;\nApex Challenges                 Fortnite Challenges\n&nbsp;\nActivity\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe activity section displays live and upcoming challenges, challenge results, and allows you to manage your cash rewards. \n&nbsp;\nApex Challenges                 Fortnite Challenges\n&nbsp;\nSo there you have it, our new Player Profiles! With that goal in mind, weve taken the most important aspects in the game and added them to a weighted formula to figure out each players rating. href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Ffortnite\u002F?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_medium=fortnite&amp;utm_campaign=dt-rankings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: rating. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-4820\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fwp-content\u002Fuploads\u002F2019\u002F10\u002FDT-ratings-1400560_01_1572007644293_Hkl4Jk_lcS.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1400\" height=\"560\" \u002F\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThe ability to survive in any Battle Royale is critical, so placement in matches is one of the important elements of the formula. If youre alive longer, theres a much higher chance that your wins, kills, and experience levels will also be elevated.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EYour fighting skills are also crucial to being considered a great player, so kills per minute is included in the rating calculation. Even if your team doesnt always win or survive the entire match, your ability to put enemies down is one of the most important factors in determining your skill.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EWhile hot-dropping is fun and chaotic and can lead to a lot of kills, its just not everyones style of play. So, kills per death is also factored into your rating. If you prefer to loot up and then start engaging when you have the advantage, that shows tactical awareness and skill. So, you may only get a few kills per game, but if youre winning the majority of your 1v1s, your rating will go up.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EAnd lastly, we factored in experience. This variable becomes less important the more you play, but matches played does provide some indication of your understanding of the game and its mechanics and, therefore, cant be overlooked. Experience is heavily front-loaded, meaning that vast improvements are made from the moment you install the game up to a certain level. After attaining a mid-to-high level, improvement still occurs but at a slower pace. So experience means less in the formula the higher you go.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003ESince Fortnite is cross-platform, and each has its own strengths and weaknesses, we want to get the most accurate rating for you on your gaming platform of choice. So, our rating will compare you to only others that play on the medium that you use. That means that if you play on mobile, your rating wont be affected by PC players who may be able to get more kills with a mouse and keyboard. If you play on multiple devices, well calculate your weighted average across all of them.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThe DreamTeam Rating is on a scale of one to ten, with a \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Ffortnite\u002Fleaderboards\u002F?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_medium=fortnite&amp;utm_campaign=dt-rankings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"\u003EDreamTeam Rating\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of five being an average player.  \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe post \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Ffortnite-dt-rating-explained\u002F\"\u003EFortnite DT Rating Explained\u003C\u002Fa\u003E appeared first on \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\"\u003EDreamTeam Blog\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n","content_text":"Your DreamTeam Rating for Fortnite is a unique feature that aims to objectively calculate a players skill level compared to all other users on a given platform (PC, console, or mobile). With that goal in mind, weve taken the most important aspects in the game and added them to a weighted formula to figure out each players rating. See your DT rating now by registering or logging onto DreamTeam.gg or continue reading to see what is taken into consideration while calculating your DT rating. \n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe ability to survive in any Battle Royale is critical, so placement in matches is one of the important elements of the formula. If youre alive longer, theres a much higher chance that your wins, kills, and experience levels will also be elevated.\n&nbsp;\nYour fighting skills are also crucial to being considered a great player, so kills per minute is included in the rating calculation. Even if your team doesnt always win or survive the entire match, your ability to put enemies down is one of the most important factors in determining your skill.\n&nbsp;\nWhile hot-dropping is fun and chaotic and can lead to a lot of kills, its just not everyones style of play. So, kills per death is also factored into your rating. If you prefer to loot up and then start engaging when you have the advantage, that shows tactical awareness and skill. So, you may only get a few kills per game, but if youre winning the majority of your 1v1s, your rating will go up.\n&nbsp;\nAnd lastly, we factored in experience. This variable becomes less important the more you play, but matches played does provide some indication of your understanding of the game and its mechanics and, therefore, cant be overlooked. Experience is heavily front-loaded, meaning that vast improvements are made from the moment you install the game up to a certain level. After attaining a mid-to-high level, improvement still occurs but at a slower pace. So experience means less in the formula the higher you go.\n&nbsp;\nSince Fortnite is cross-platform, and each has its own strengths and weaknesses, we want to get the most accurate rating for you on your gaming platform of choice. So, our rating will compare you to only others that play on the medium that you use. That means that if you play on mobile, your rating wont be affected by PC players who may be able to get more kills with a mouse and keyboard. If you play on multiple devices, well calculate your weighted average across all of them.\n&nbsp;\nThe DreamTeam Rating is on a scale of one to ten, with a DreamTeam Rating of five being an average player.  \nThe post Fortnite DT Rating Explained appeared first on DreamTeam Blog.","date_published":"2019-10-25T15:57:51+00:00","date_modified":"2019-11-13T16:12:42+00:00","author":{"name":"Jacob \"KnowWear\" Brubaker","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fauthor\u002Fjacob-knowwear-brubaker\u002F","avatar":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fwp-content\u002Fuploads\u002F2018\u002F11\u002Favatar_user_6_1543503233-512x512.png"},"image":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fwp-content\u002Fuploads\u002F2019\u002F10\u002FNew-Project-29.png"},"the-most-advanced-lfg":{"id":"the-most-advanced-lfg","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fthe-most-advanced-lfg\u002F","title":"The Most Advanced LFG","content_html":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003ESo youve just come home and wanna play some Fortnite. Heres how:\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch3 style=\"text-align: center;\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003ENew Post Algorithm\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003E \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EOur LFG no longer displays posts based on time posted. GL HF!\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe post \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fthe-most-advanced-lfg\u002F\"\u003EThe Most Advanced LFG\u003C\u002Fa\u003E appeared first on \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\"\u003EDreamTeam Blog\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n","content_text":"So youve just come home and wanna play some Fortnite. And wouldnt you know it, none of your Fortnite friends are online. Its been a long day and you really dont feel like playing with toxic randoms. We understand your pain. We gotcha. Visit the DreamTeam.gg LFG and, boom, problem solved. \n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThe latest LFG update makes finding a duo or squad even easier and faster. Heres how:\n&nbsp;\nNew Post Algorithm \n&nbsp;\nOur LFG no longer displays posts based on time posted. Although doing that is helpful, it isnt really what is most important to players who use our LFG feature. The DreamTeam LFG now displays posts based on who is currently online first. After all, thats what really matters. Players use LFG to find someone to play with at that moment. So, players no longer need to scroll through posts to find the players who are currently online or wait until an offline player replies to a message. Players can connect and start playing sooner. As an added bonus, weve also added a spam filter. Say goodbye to pointless posts forever. \n&nbsp;\nFIND PLAYERS\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nQuick Skill Understanding\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nEach post displays the most important piece of information related to a players skill: the DreamTeam Rating. The DreamTeam rating uses a complex algorithm to calculate a players overall skill based on stats and play experience. If you are looking for a player and have a DT Rating of 8.5, you can quickly understand that its probably a waste of time to reply to a post of a player who has a DT rating of 0.6. \n&nbsp;\nVIEW RATINGS\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nFilter System\n    \n&nbsp;\nYou can now quickly filter the LFG post by platform, mic, and, most importantly, game mode. We know every player has a favorite game mode. And yes, we have excluded Solo for obvious reasons . \n&nbsp;\nUSE FILTERS\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nSharing \n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nYou now have the ability to share that you are looking for players across Facebook groups and Twitter. Hopefully, you shouldnt need this as our LFG finds players pretty quickly. However, we would appreciate a share or two for some advertising. Wink. Wink.\nSHARE A POST\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nAvatar\n&nbsp;\nWeve also added avatars. Youve chosen your avatar for a reason. Why not attach it to your post? Done. Each post now displays a little bit more about who the poster is. \n&nbsp;\nThats it for the latest LFG update. Now get out there and create a post. For example &#8211; everyone having a shot at that first elimination or Victory Royale moment and the satisfying feeling that comes with it. Right now, we know there are players out there who have never had that opportunity.\n&nbsp;\n\n&nbsp;\nThis seems to point to an increased focus on bringing in new players or getting gamers who are just starting off to commit to the game. Whether this is an attempt to get newer players to start playing for longer and having more fun or a decision made based on their sales funnel (probably the latter), the outrage from the more competitive players has risen to new highs.\n&nbsp;\nEven this week as Apex Legends released its new Solo mode, one of the top voted posts on the Apex Legends subreddit was about Fortnite players coming over to join because they were frustrated with EPIC not listening to their concerns. Ninja is a household name, not just in esports but in pop culture. The worlds most popular gamer has used his talents and the popularity of Fortnite to gain a massive cult following. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003ETwitch is basically the only name in streaming video games. Out of the top five most-popular game streaming platforms (twitch, Mixer, Youtube Gaming, Periscope, and Facebook Live), Twitch had 69% of the total concurrent viewers of all the channels combined.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EUntil yesterday, it was hard to imagine the two ever separating.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThen Mixer stepped in. The details of the agreement between Ninja and Mixer havent been disclosed, but theres a very high probability that the money thrown his way must be astronomical. Theres surely guaranteed money that isnt dependant on subscribers or viewership numbers which is likely enough for Ninja to live off of for a long time.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EIn 2018, dotesports calculated that Ninja was making more than \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdotesports.com\u002Fnews\u002Fhow-much-money-does-ninja-make-21954\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003E$658,000 per month\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003E from twitch subscribers alone. And during that year, he is said to have made more than $10 million from subscribers, donations, advertisements, and sponsorships. But, that number is a low-ball estimate. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThis is clearly a massive effort to attract more gaming fans to Mixer. And, less than 24 hours after the deal was announced, Mixer is number one on the App Store for downloads. This experiment will be the first real test of how loyal fans are to a particular streamer or if they prefer the ease and comfortability of a particular platform. So, the long-term benefits of this test will be reaped by almost everyone in the streaming world. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\n\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EIf Ninja brings his fans with him, streamers will have the upper hand in negotiating with platforms. But, if twitch maintains its market share, platforms will be forced to drastically improve their products and marketing to gain a solid footing in the ever-growing live-streaming sphere.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe post \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Ffortnites-biggest-star-ninja-leaves-twitch-for-mixer\u002F\"\u003EFortnites Biggest Star, Ninja Leaves Twitch For Mixer\u003C\u002Fa\u003E appeared first on \u003Ca rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\"\u003EDreamTeam Blog\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n","content_text":"Fortnites Biggest Star, Ninja leaves twitch for Mixer\n&nbsp;\nTyler Ninja Blevins has announced that hes signed an exclusive streaming deal with Mixer, Microsofts streaming service. Ninja is a household name, not just in esports but in pop culture. The worlds most popular gamer has used his talents and the popularity of Fortnite to gain a massive cult following. \n&nbsp;\nTwitch is basically the only name in streaming video games. Out of the top five most-popular game streaming platforms (twitch, Mixer, Youtube Gaming, Periscope, and Facebook Live), Twitch had 69% of the total concurrent viewers of all the channels combined.\n&nbsp;\nUntil yesterday, it was hard to imagine the two ever separating.\n&nbsp;\nThen Mixer stepped in. The details of the agreement between Ninja and Mixer havent been disclosed, but theres a very high probability that the money thrown his way must be astronomical. Theres surely guaranteed money that isnt dependant on subscribers or viewership numbers which is likely enough for Ninja to live off of for a long time.\n&nbsp;\nIn 2018, dotesports calculated that Ninja was making more than $658,000 per month from twitch subscribers alone. And during that year, he is said to have made more than $10 million from subscribers, donations, advertisements, and sponsorships. But, that number is a low-ball estimate. \n&nbsp;\nThis is clearly a massive effort to attract more gaming fans to Mixer. And, less than 24 hours after the deal was announced, Mixer is number one on the App Store for downloads. This experiment will be the first real test of how loyal fans are to a particular streamer or if they prefer the ease and comfortability of a particular platform. So, the long-term benefits of this test will be reaped by almost everyone in the streaming world. \n\nIf Ninja brings his fans with him, streamers will have the upper hand in negotiating with platforms. But, if twitch maintains its market share, platforms will be forced to drastically improve their products and marketing to gain a solid footing in the ever-growing live-streaming sphere.\nThe post Fortnites Biggest Star, Ninja Leaves Twitch For Mixer appeared first on DreamTeam Blog.","date_published":"2019-08-02T12:38:49+00:00","date_modified":"2019-08-02T12:39:28+00:00","author":{"name":"Kellen \"Legend\" Derry","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fauthor\u002Fkellen-legend-derry\u002F","avatar":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fwp-content\u002Fuploads\u002F2018\u002F11\u002Favatar_user_3_1543499511.png"},"image":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fwp-content\u002Fuploads\u002F2019\u002F08\u002FNinja-leaves-Twitch-for-Mixer-in-the-first-big-shot-of-livestreamings-content-war.jpg"},"teen-kyle-bugha-giersdorf-wins-fortnite-world-cup-takes-home-3-million":{"id":"teen-kyle-bugha-giersdorf-wins-fortnite-world-cup-takes-home-3-million","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fdreamteam.gg\u002Fblog\u002Fteen-kyle-bugha-giersdorf-wins-fortnite-world-cup-takes-home-3-million\u002F","title":"Teen, Kyle Bugha Giersdorf Wins Fortnite World Cup, Takes Home $3 Million","content_html":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThis was the week of the teenagers in New York. On consecutive days, players not old enough to vote took their positions on top of the gaming world by winning both the Duos and Solos tournaments at the Fortnite World Cup. The biggest prize went to Pennsylvania native, Kyle Bugha Giersdorf, who was able to sweep aside some of the worlds strongest competitors without breaking too much of a sweat.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch3\u003E\u003Cb\u003ESolos\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EAt a sold-out Arthur Ashe Stadium in Flushing, New York, the fight for the biggest prize pool in esports history (at least until The International crowns a champion in a few weeks) gave fans some of the highest-level play in competitive gaming. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EIn the six-game series, Bugha was able to string together solid performance and solid performance, even getting a Victory Royale in the opening game. He played aggressively, leading from the front the entire way and had the title locked up with a game to spare. \u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EAfter being the first to qualify for the event from the North America East region way back in April, Bugha began working tirelessly on a training regimen. ESPN reported that he would practice 8-10 hours a day, eat a specific Wawa sandwich and Gatorade before important online matches. On Sunday, he was without the staples of his diet. And, he still managed to win convincingly.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch3\u003E\u003Cb\u003EDuos\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003ENorwegian, Emil Bergquist Pedersen and Austrian, David W, also known as Nyhrox and Aqua  took home the first-place trophy in the Duos tournament on Saturday. Their victory netted them $1.5 million each and crowned them champions in the first-ever Fortnite World Cup.\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003EThe pair were able to dominate the high ground and finish strongly after a less-than-optimal start. On consecutive days, players not old enough to vote took their positions on top of the gaming world by winning both the Duos and Solos tournaments at the Fortnite World Cup. The biggest prize went to Pennsylvania native, Kyle Bugha Giersdorf, who was able to sweep aside some of the worlds strongest competitors without breaking too much of a sweat.\n&nbsp;\nSolos\n&nbsp;\nAt a sold-out Arthur Ashe Stadium in Flushing, New York, the fight for the biggest prize pool in esports history (at least until The International crowns a champion in a few weeks) gave fans some of the highest-level play in competitive gaming. \n&nbsp;\nIn the six-game series, Bugha was able to string together solid performance and solid performance, even getting a Victory Royale in the opening game. He played aggressively, leading from the front the entire way and had the title locked up with a game to spare. \n&nbsp;\nAfter being the first to qualify for the event from the North America East region way back in April, Bugha began working tirelessly on a training regimen. ESPN reported that he would practice 8-10 hours a day, eat a specific Wawa sandwich and Gatorade before important online matches. On Sunday, he was without the staples of his diet. And, he still managed to win convincingly.\n&nbsp;\nDuos\n&nbsp;\nNorwegian, Emil Bergquist Pedersen and Austrian, David W, also known as Nyhrox and Aqua  took home the first-place trophy in the Duos tournament on Saturday. Their victory netted them $1.5 million each and crowned them champions in the first-ever Fortnite World Cup.\n&nbsp;\nThe pair were able to dominate the high ground and finish strongly after a less-than-optimal start. The secured back-to-back victories in games 4 and 5, pushing them past some other really tough European competition. \n&nbsp;\nNorth America was represented well by 100 Thieves duo, Elevate and Ciece, who came in third and picked up a $1.8 million check for their efforts.\n&nbsp;\nThe competition at the Fortnite World Cup was everything a fan couldve asked for. That strategy has transformed the game from a single-player curiosity into a worldwide sensation, attracting an obscene number of players to the title. Were celebrating all over the Battle Royale map with present supply drops, birthday cakes and a gift item youll be able to toss to your squad.\nEven the Battle Bus will get some tuning, with specially-themed music now live and running until the end of the event. \n&nbsp;\nAlthough not much of a surprise, given the leaks that came about the celebration, a new pickaxe, wrap and some additional cosmetics are now available in-game.\n&nbsp;\nWorld Cup Items\n&nbsp;\nA few limited-time cosmetics commemorating the Fortnite World Cup are also there for players to enjoy. Unlike the cosmetics, these challenges will be able to be completed until the end of Season 9. The challenges will be released three at a time, every three days. Along with the solos and duos, Tyler Ninja Blevins and Marshmello will team up once again to see if they can combine for another win in the Fortnite Pro-Am event.\n&nbsp;\nHeres how you can keep up with everything going on this weekend.\n&nbsp;\n&nbsp;\nWhere to watch\n&nbsp;\nFortnite.com\nTwitch\nFacebook\nCaffeine\nMixer\nYouTube\n&nbsp;\nAn awesome new feature that Epic just introduced is picture-in-picture. While youre building or gunning your enemies down, youll be able to watch whats happening in the World Cup on the same screen on which youre playing. \n\nWhen to watch\n&nbsp;\nDepending on whats most interesting to you, Epic has scheduled four events that will take place over the weekend, so that everyone has something to watch.
